     ZIP4                              character varying(5),
     COUNTRY_CD                        character varying(5),
     DELIVERABILITY_FLG                character varying(1),
     CARRIER_ID                        character varying(5),
     ADDR_LINK                         character varying(20),
     LARGE_PRISON_FLG                  character varying(1),
     GEO_MATCH_CD                      character varying(1),
     GEO_LATITUDE                      character varying(20),
     GEO_LONGITUDE                     character varying(20),
     GEO_FIPS_STATE                    character varying(2),
     GEO_FIPS_COUNTY                   character varying(3),
     GEO_TRACT                         character varying(6),
     GEO_BLOCK                         character varying(4),
     GEO_FIPS_MCD                      character varying(5),
     GEO_FIPS_PLACE                    character varying(5),
     GEO_CBSA                          character varying(5),
     GEO_DMA_CD                        character varying(5),
     GEO_AC_NIELSEN_COUNTY_CD          character varying(1)
)
DISTRIBUTE ON (PRI_ADDR, ADDR_LINK, ZIP_CD, CITY_NM)
